<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1f2c16da-a76e-4c34-8236-c353ffde2b4b'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<div id="review_1430055475" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1430055475" />
    <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson"><img alt="Whitney Atkinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550868411p2/14457130.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1430055475?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Atkinson" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson">Whitney Atkinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=memoir">memoir</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1430055475" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7751256917905248106">3.5<br/><br/>I'm veeerrryyy torn about this book... My biggest advice would probably be, don't look into this book unless you reeeally like Tyler Oakley. The writing in this book makes it seem like he's narrating this to a 12 year-old who's obsessed with him. It's not necessarily condescending, but he narrates his life very . . . I don't even know. Entitled. Along with that, the writing itself isn't the absolute best, and many times is a bit corny. He writes exactly how he speaks in his videos-- slang and</span>
  <span id="freeText7751256917905248106" style="display:none">3.5<br /><br />I'm veeerrryyy torn about this book... My biggest advice would probably be, don't look into this book unless you reeeally like Tyler Oakley. The writing in this book makes it seem like he's narrating this to a 12 year-old who's obsessed with him. It's not necessarily condescending, but he narrates his life very . . . I don't even know. Entitled. Along with that, the writing itself isn't the absolute best, and many times is a bit corny. He writes exactly how he speaks in his videos-- slang and puns and all-- and I can't help but think that this book would have been a more entertaining video than it was a book. The main reasons I bought this are because 1) I do think Tyler is a charming and silly person, and I wanted to support him, and 2) He kept selling this book as "stories i've never spoken about before," and that really intrigued me. I will say that this book revealed a lot about Tyler that I would have never guessed (such as his real first name isn't even Tyler, but you'll have to read the book to find that out), so it delivered what I expected. Even so, I can't help but feeling like this book just seemed like such Entitlement. The only reason it exists is because he's famous. If Tyler Oakley was some random person on the street, he wouldn't narrate a book like this or be able to sell millions of copies without a fanbase. Without his fame, this book would be completely irrelevant and probably boring. So that's why I'd only recommend this to people who are Tyler fans, and within that group of people, only those who are younger, since his writing is a bit lame and tailored toward younger people. (An afterthought: that's actually a weird way for me to promote this book because it was actually quite inappropriate at times, too. I guess just look up the first chapter of this on Amazon preview and decide for yourself how the narration sits with you.)<br /><br />This was the first book I've picked up from a big Youtuber, and I don't expect i'll buy one again unless, again, it's a person that I REALLY support. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7751256917905248106" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1435780824" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1435780824" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394406877p2/2473504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1435780824?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=listened-to-audiobook">listened-to-audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=nonfiction">nonfiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=lgbtq">lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=memoir-biography-autobiography">memoir-biography-autobiography</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=stand-alone-novel">stand-alone-novel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1435780824" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3259157666646609216">There are very few YouTube channels I follow and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8301425.Tyler_Oakley' title='Tyler Oakley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tyler Oakley</a>'s isn't one of them. It's not because I don't like him though...I just never heard of him before. I know, where have I been hiding??? <br/><br/>While waiting for my next library hold, I saw <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25507925.Binge' title='Binge by Tyler Oakley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Binge</a> was readily available via audio. It was categorized as humor so why wouldn't I read something mood lifting? I ended up really liking it...and really liking Tyler. From my reading experience, I can honestly say Tyler's book is enjoyable whether you are </span>
  <span id="freeText3259157666646609216" style="display:none">There are very few YouTube channels I follow and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8301425.Tyler_Oakley" title="Tyler Oakley" rel="nofollow noopener">Tyler Oakley</a>'s isn't one of them. It's not because I don't like him though...I just never heard of him before. I know, where have I been hiding??? <br /><br />While waiting for my next library hold, I saw <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25507925.Binge" title="Binge by Tyler Oakley" rel="nofollow noopener">Binge</a> was readily available via audio. It was categorized as humor so why wouldn't I read something mood lifting? I ended up really liking it...and really liking Tyler. From my reading experience, I can honestly say Tyler's book is enjoyable whether you are familiar with him or not. Regardless, I feel like I know him now and I might even consider checking out his channel, so if that was an underlying reason behind this book then it worked. <br /><br />Tyler writes with substance as well as plenty of humor. He discusses his experiences with eating disorders, suicidal thoughts, abusive relationships, coming out to a religious parent, advocacy, and his slow rise to fame in the world of social media. Tyler shared that he wrote <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25507925.Binge" title="Binge by Tyler Oakley" rel="nofollow noopener">Binge</a> with the wish to demonstrate "the value of taking chances, pushing beyond our comfort levels, dusting ourselves off after our inevitable humiliations, and remaining open to the life and feelings and possibilities that are happening while we are busy either chasing phantoms of success or trying to outrun our fears." Personally, I think he succeeded.<br /><br />The audiobook version of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25507925.Binge" title="Binge by Tyler Oakley" rel="nofollow noopener">Binge</a> was a fun experience for me. Tyler self-narrated and spoke directly to the listener, even letting the reader know if there was a screenshot or something they were visually missing in which case he tried to summarize/describe it the best he could. The audio was well-done in my opinion and I would recommend it. Check it out!<br /><br /><b>My favorite quotes:</b><br /><i>"A good mom is supportive of you but the best moms are supportive of your growth. Even when it doesn't seem like they're on your side, great mothers are on the side of your becoming a better person and you'll be so much better off in the long run. So pull out your flip phone and text a quick thank you to your mom. She has your best interest at heart even if you are sometimes a dick."</i><br /><br /><b>Note:</b> So who is Tyler Oakley? He is a strong presence on YouTube and all of the social media outlets. At the time of this review, he has 7,737,335 YouTube subscribers, 5.3m Instagram followers, 4.75M Twitter followers, 2,811,812 Facebook likes, and an impressive number of Snapchat and Tumblr fans. He has this book (obviously) as well as an upcoming documentary titled Snervous set to release December 2015. After some research, I learned that Tyler is not only a social media obsession but he is also an advocate for LGBT rights and <a href="http://www.thetrevorproject.org/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Trevor Project</a>, an organization that provides crisis intervention and suicide prevention services to LGBTQ youth ages 13-24. I have to admit, I find it impressive that Tyler uses his popularity and influence to do good. Keep up the good work Tyler!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3259157666646609216" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Paige  Bookdragon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15550986-paige-bookdragon"><img alt="Paige  Bookdragon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570121828p2/15550986.jpg" /></a>

  <span id="freeText589218891031269467" style="display:none"><blockquote> <b> <i> The rectum is a grand thing.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm not a fan of Tyler and I'm also not a hater. I've heard of him, yes, but I never followed him on social media because:<br><br>1. I don't have twitter because who am I going to tweet and what am I going to say?<br><br><b>
  <i> I'm off to @Starbucks, guys! #frappe #latte </i>
</b><br><br>Please. I'd rather dieeee.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446483466ra/16815203.gif" width="500" height="286" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and 2. I mostly watch funny cats in youtube, and Tyler doesn't have those.<br><br>But I bought his book and decided to read it because if I can buy pervy books, why not buy funny books like this?<br><br>So I read it and I gotta say, <b> THIS IS ABSOLUTELY FUNNY AND REAL.</b> Basically, Tyler talks about himself and usually, I find that annoying to a person but weirdly, I like him because he is just so unapologetically proud of his self and I admire that to a person.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446483466ra/16815204.gif" width="448" height="243" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And did I mention his words of wisdom is so cute?<br><br><blockquote> <b> <i> “Listen, your asshole is precious. I love the way Tyler talks about love,relationships, his family, anxiety, insecurity and violence. I like the way he didn't make himself just the victim. He acknowledges he has some faults in it and I think that's wonderful. <br><br>So, Binge + Me= Wonderful moments.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446483466ra/16815207.gif" width="470" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9159642526548613943"><b>Tyler Oakley is already one of the most beautiful human beings on the planet.</b><br/><a href='https://49.media.tumblr.com/281116fdb74aac4dd4e85876e6ef4c8e/tumblr_nixeehlh5L1tloylpo1_400.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/>But <i>Binge</i> takes your love for him to a whole new level. It's a bundle of refreshing honesty, laugh-your-head-off comedy, and heartfelt pearls of wisdom that is hard to put down. <br/><br/>The best part? The personal feel of it all - it's almost as personal as watching one of his videos. Reading this book feels like you're delving into someone else's mind, thoughts...their life. Never one to sugarcoat, Tyler writes about the g</span>
  <span id="freeText9159642526548613943" style="display:none"><b>Tyler Oakley is already one of the most beautiful human beings on the planet.</b><br><a href="https://49.media.tumblr.com/281116fdb74aac4dd4e85876e6ef4c8e/tumblr_nixeehlh5L1tloylpo1_400.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450398388ra/17420458.gif" alt="https://49.media.tumblr.com/281116fdb74aac4dd4e85876e6ef4c8e/tumblr_nixeehlh5L1tloylpo1_400.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>But <i>Binge</i> takes your love for him to a whole new level. It's a bundle of refreshing honesty, laugh-your-head-off comedy, and heartfelt pearls of wisdom that is hard to put down. <br><br>The best part? The personal feel of it all - it's almost as personal as watching one of his videos. Reading this book feels like you're delving into someone else's mind, thoughts...their life. Never one to sugarcoat, Tyler writes about the good, the bad, the ugly, and the downright awesome in a book that is certainly one you can binge-read to your heart's content!</span>

<div id="review_1885611665" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1885611665" />
    <a title="Mrs.Morgan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34425339-mrs-morgan"><img alt="Mrs.Morgan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483106116p2/34425339.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1885611665?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mrs.Morgan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mrs.Morgan" href="/user/show/34425339-mrs-morgan">Mrs.Morgan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1885611665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12231770739612813588">It was relatively interesting how I came by this book: my students were involved in a biography unit and I kept hearing <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8301425.Tyler_Oakley' title='Tyler Oakley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tyler Oakley</a>'s name come up and seeing his book carried about. When I asked a few kids about it, they <b>
  <u>raved</u>
</b> about him. (There are fewer ways to make me feel old and not nearly as cool as I used to be than to start talking about some <i>YouTube sensation</i> that I have never seen or heard of .. [what is the point of YouTube anyway?!]).<br/><br/>Anyway, I knew I needed to acquire this book t</span>
  <span id="freeText12231770739612813588" style="display:none">It was relatively interesting how I came by this book: my students were involved in a biography unit and I kept hearing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8301425.Tyler_Oakley" title="Tyler Oakley" rel="nofollow noopener">Tyler Oakley</a>'s name come up and seeing his book carried about. When I asked a few kids about it, they <b>
  <u>raved</u>
</b> about him. (There are fewer ways to make me feel old and not nearly as cool as I used to be than to start talking about some <i>YouTube sensation</i> that I have never seen or heard of .. [what is the point of YouTube anyway?!]).<br /><br />Anyway, I knew I needed to acquire this book to figure out what all the fuss was about. After all, my students getting excited about a biography is too good to be true!<br /><br />Imagine my surprise when I received Oakley's book in the mail and I happened upon a sentence as I was casually flipping through the book that made me immediately decide that I had to read this myself AND find him on YouTube, stat. <br /><br />What I found on YouTube was engaging, humorous, and REAL! Watching him was fun and I wanted in on that fun -- (it helped that the video I watched was him interacting with Kristen Bell, one of my favorite people on Earth). Needless to say, the same can be mentioned about his book. I will err on the side of Oakley being a little <i>too</i> honest but his book makes you want to live vicariously through his life and his experiences (for the most part). Walking away, if nothing else, I wanted him as a friend or to at least find a friend <i>like</i> him!<br /><br />Having gone from a person whom I had never even heard of before, to watching some videos that he did and reading his autobiography and [mostly] loving it, I would say that [Mathew] Tyler Oakley is quite captivating and his book is worth the read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12231770739612813588" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4247940-abby?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4247940-abby?shelf=memoir">memoir</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1405262111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2045207086731103468">Tyler Oakley’s debut memoir <i>Binge</i> brings readers behind the camera of his popular YouTube videos. We learn about his childhood, his rankings of Disney Prince hottness, and the wild ride he’s had since hitting Youtube fame– and more! The chapters of <i>Binge</i> could all stand on their own as essays, but are woven together over the course of the book to give readers the perfect mix of raw honesty and hilarious absurdity.<br/><br/>I am in awe at the impressive levels of internal and external reflections with whic</span>
  <span id="freeText2045207086731103468" style="display:none">Tyler Oakley’s debut memoir <i>Binge</i> brings readers behind the camera of his popular YouTube videos. We learn about his childhood, his rankings of Disney Prince hottness, and the wild ride he’s had since hitting Youtube fame– and more! The chapters of <i>Binge</i> could all stand on their own as essays, but are woven together over the course of the book to give readers the perfect mix of raw honesty and hilarious absurdity.<br /><br />I am in awe at the impressive levels of internal and external reflections with which Oakley approaches his life. Instead of simply telling his story, he truly pulls the reader in, diving into the intimidating nature of vulnerability and reflects on dark topics, such as his experiences with an eating disorder and physical abuse. He outwardly acknowledges the unique platform he has grown and states his goal of using it to bring awareness to various topics and help his (primarily teen) audience members who are struggling.<br /><br />On a more technical note, Oakley impeccably translates his charismatic, onversatonal tone from his videos to this book. I felt as though I could hear him speaking the words I was writing on the page!<br /><br />Hands down, five stars. An incredible memoir and reflection of the newfound internet culture and its resulting fame.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2045207086731103468" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15443159904108461845" style="display:none">I guess I should mention that I love Youtube (and the internet as a whole). I follow Book channels, Art channels, Spirituality, Business, Movies and I think a lot of people will agree - it's far better than watching the TV! But apart from the occasional PewdiePie video, I don't really know much about the celebrities on the network. <br /><br /><i>Do you need to be a Tyler Oakley fan in order to enjoy his book? </i><br />Short answer - No. I've only seen a couple of his videos prior to reading his book (and a few more after finishing it). <br /><br />Why did I read it? I was curious, I wanted to understand the hype and the pop culture of the younger generation. <br /><br />Was it phenomenally amazing? - Ummmm....not for me, but we all have our own preferences. <br /><br />Anyways, Binge is a funny, heart-warming and entertaining read. I wasn't mind-blown by it, but I did relate to Tyler and I did feel for him in almost every story. Check it out if you are a fan of his or if you're just curious about the current trends in the Youtube community. The book also offers a great deal of information about what it takes to be successful Youtuber and let me tell you - I'll go mad after only a week. If people like Tyler and Pewdiepie can go through such a torture every day, than they deserve every bit of their fame and money.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15443159904108461845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1330517536" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1330517536" />
    <a title="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33425898-courtney-librarycutie"><img alt="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597323627p2/33425898.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1330517536?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Courtney ♡ librarycutie" href="/user/show/33425898-courtney-librarycutie">Courtney ♡ librarycutie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33425898-courtney-librarycutie?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33425898-courtney-librarycutie?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33425898-courtney-librarycutie?shelf=memoirs">memoirs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1330517536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14025602796803165173">review on blog: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://librarycutie.wordpress.com/2015/12/22/review-binge-by-tyler-oakley/'>https://librarycutie.wordpress.com/20...</a><br/><br/>If you’ve been following me on Instagram or Twitter then you know i’ve been in a really depressing book slump for the past few months so i’ve decided to listen to Tyler Oakley’s new book Binge, narrated by the queen himself. Saying I loved it is definitely an understatement. It was phenomenal! Tyler, you’ve not only booted my sad emotions to being more happier and positive, but i’m also considering buying your book too, just to have in case</span>
  <span id="freeText14025602796803165173" style="display:none">review on blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://librarycutie.wordpress.com/2015/12/22/review-binge-by-tyler-oakley/">https://librarycutie.wordpress.com/20...</a><br /><br />If you’ve been following me on Instagram or Twitter then you know i’ve been in a really depressing book slump for the past few months so i’ve decided to listen to Tyler Oakley’s new book Binge, narrated by the queen himself. Saying I loved it is definitely an understatement. It was phenomenal! Tyler, you’ve not only booted my sad emotions to being more happier and positive, but i’m also considering buying your book too, just to have in case i want to read it again.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I aggressively run into things, back up into things, have no depth perception, often forget which buttons and knobs do what, and am easily distracted. But enough about my sex life! Back to my driving skills!”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br />Let me say, I’ve been watching Tyler’s videos for a while, maybe four years, I can’t exactly pin point it but probably 3-4. I remember tweeting “who is tyler oakley?” because I was in the One Direction fandom or something, and he was all over the fandom news, and he FAVED IT! I laughed, and didn’t realize that I would soon be in love with that adorable cupcake.<br /><br />But really, Who is Tyler Oakley? Sure, his life mainly consists on the internet, but what do we know about his personal life? Not a whole life, once you think about it. In this Memior Binge, we get a huge look into Matthew’s life, and who he really is, and what made him who he is today!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Tyler Oakley isn’t my real name.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br />binge-is-finally-here-01Since I listened to the book on Audible, I’ll rate the performance… can I give it a 100 out of 100 or no? Okay, 5/5 stars! It’s was such a great book, It felt as though Tyler himself was talking directly to me. I felt so involved that I didn’t want to stop listening to it. You get to see the personal and almost secret side of Matthew Tyler Oakley.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“No person, no matter how important society deems their relationship to you, has the right to denounce you for who you are.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br />Not only was this book hilarious, but it was also inspiring and important. Tyler talks about his struggles with an eating disorder, and about his struggle about coming out and how it was hard for his dad to accept it, and the struggles of dating someone who hasn’t accepted themselves. Life isn’t perfect, especially for the adorable and internationally known internet star Tyler Oakley. He lets it all out, literally. I about died when he was talking about driving just to hook up with this guy.. I’m actually cracking up thinking back on it. The audio book is 10 times better than the book, simply because you get to hear Tyler himself, and it’s the best thing ever. His voice expresses everything, and it just connects you with the book in a way you can’t with the book. So, get both!<br /><br />I also want to thank Tyler for the truth he has shown in this book, he’s such a brave guy putting all this out in the open, and I hope e knows this book is a masterpiece, and it’s definitely helped me with so much. Not only did it cheer me up, but it helped me see things much clearer. Also, can we please appreciate bi-curious people because they do exist, thanks! I feel like that, among other things, is something that stuck out most, his appreciation for the LGBTQ+ community, and how he’s really helping everyone in that community with this book.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“This is why homophobia is a terrible evil: it disguises itself as concern while it is inherently hate.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br />I’m not even sure what I was expecting out of this, but it definitely exceeded my expectations by a landslide, I think this made me love Tyler even more! He’s such a unique person, and we all need to enjoy his admirable personality, and just give this memoir a chance. If you barely know anything about Tyler, then i’m pretty sure you would still enjoy the humor and honesty from this book, there’s no doubt you won’t laugh. How can you not appreciate Tyler for speaking out about what he’s dealt with, struggled deeply with, and tried to keep in the past. He’s so real, and he’s so proud of himself that I greatly admire that, and that’s one of the reasons this memoir was so inspiring, because Tyler has inspired me.<br /><br />Okay, I will admit a lot of weird shit is discussed in this book, in between the deep personal topics, but that’s Tyler, that’s what to expect form him, you just… go along with it.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Binge on giving, in all senses. Binge on indulging. We’re told every day from an early age that moderation is key. Count your calories, wait a while before you tell someone you love them, and remember that balance is the path to happiness. While all of those are great in theory, does a lesson taught from someone else’s mistakes resonate just as deeply as the ones you learn yourself? When you binge, you find your own boundaries.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br />Anyways, If you’re a fan of Tyler Oakley, then why haven’t you read/listened to it yet? You so need to, I recommend the audio if you can, you’ll thank me later. I apologize if this review is so short, I could;t put my thoughts and emotions in any coherent sentences, I just really enjoyed this and I recommend it.<br /><br />Tyler, my twitter is <i>@coffeesphan</i><br />xx Courtney</span>
  <a data-text-id="14025602796803165173" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1322465897" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15035682000897192168"><u>
  <i>I read this book for the BookTubeAThon 2017 (Challenge #3: Read about a character that is very different from you)</i>
</u><br/><br/><b>"When life throws a wrench in your plans, catch it and build an IKEA bookshelf."</b><br/><br/>Tyler seriously cannot disappoint me!<br/><br/>When this book was announced and, later, when it actually came out in print, I had my mind set on getting a physical copy of it. And then other things came between me and actually getting the damn book. So I decided to listen to it as an audio book instead.<br/><br/><i>I WAS NO</i></span>
  <span id="freeText15035682000897192168" style="display:none"><u>
  <i>I read this book for the BookTubeAThon 2017 (Challenge #3: Read about a character that is very different from you)</i>
</u><br /><br /><b>"When life throws a wrench in your plans, catch it and build an IKEA bookshelf."</b><br /><br />Tyler seriously cannot disappoint me!<br /><br />When this book was announced and, later, when it actually came out in print, I had my mind set on getting a physical copy of it. And then other things came between me and actually getting the damn book. So I decided to listen to it as an audio book instead.<br /><br /><i>I WAS NOT DISAPPOINTED!</i><br /><br />Tyler reads this book himself - and adds comments, questions and other things just for the listeners. Which does make this audio book feel like you're sitting in the same room as him, just listening to him telling his stories. Because, comments and questions and other things are sweet and all, but they do not measure up to the stories.<br /><br />I didn't start actively following Tyler Oakley until about three years ago, around the time when I was doing my last semester at university. Sure, I knew who he was and had watched a few of his videos prior to that, but that was when I actually subscribed and started watching <i>everything</i> he uploaded.<br /><br />However, videos lasting a few minutes can only tell so much. In this book, Tyler tells longer stories, more intricate ones, ones that he has sometimes only mentioned in passing but never delved into properly, or ones he has not touched at all. It's pure and real, funny and sad, and it doesn't take roundabout routes to point out the truth.<br /><br />Two words; read it. Read this book. Right now!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1425735463" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6619353167528264016">I am more of a casual Tyler Oakley fan. I watch his videos from time to time, I enjoy them most of the time but I can't say I adooooooore him. <br/><br/>Having said that, I really really really liked this book. I think a big part in me liking it so much is the fact that I actually listened to it. And I think that is the best way to experience this "story". Tyler narrates it of course and that's what made it for me. It feels just like listening to one of his videos: it's fun and energetic, sometimes emotio</span>
  <span id="freeText6619353167528264016" style="display:none">I am more of a casual Tyler Oakley fan. I watch his videos from time to time, I enjoy them most of the time but I can't say I adooooooore him. <br /><br />Having said that, I really really really liked this book. I think a big part in me liking it so much is the fact that I actually listened to it. And I think that is the best way to experience this "story". Tyler narrates it of course and that's what made it for me. It feels just like listening to one of his videos: it's fun and energetic, sometimes emotional and always engaging. There wasn't a single moment when I felt bored or annoyed. <br />The fact that he is really good at talking about himself and his life shouldn't be surprising seeing as he made an actual career out of it. <br /><br />In the end, I can't say I agree with everything he says/does etc. but that doesn't really matter. This isn't about agreeing with him, it's about appreciating his work and in my opinion he did a very very good job.</span>

<div id="review_1637859904" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1637859904" />
    <a title="Yvonne (bookishpanda)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4023744-yvonne-bookishpanda"><img alt="Yvonne (bookishpanda)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454500294p2/4023744.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1637859904?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Yvonne (bookishpanda)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Yvonne (bookishpanda)" href="/user/show/4023744-yvonne-bookishpanda">Yvonne (bookishpanda)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4023744-yvonne-bookishpanda?shelf=ebooks-i-own">ebooks-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4023744-yvonne-bookishpanda?shelf=4-stars-books">4-stars-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4023744-yvonne-bookishpanda?shelf=stand-alones">stand-alones</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1637859904" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11484932832997457699"><a href='http://aworldbetweenfoldedpages.blogspot.co.at/2016/08/review-binge-by-tyler-oakley.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452000576i/17631522.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I've loved Tyler ever since I saw one of his videos on Youtube. There's just something so incredibly <i>captivating </i>about him ... he's adorable, funny and besides that he's also very inspiring and creative. This book proves just as much - <b>he shares intimate stories with his readers/viewers and talks openly about the things he learned in life.</b> His school time, relationships, casual hook-ups, his internet presence, different jobs he's had over the years and so much more.<br/><br/>I have to admit, I never r</span>
  <span id="freeText11484932832997457699" style="display:none"><a href="http://aworldbetweenfoldedpages.blogspot.co.at/2016/08/review-binge-by-tyler-oakley.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452000576i/17631522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I've loved Tyler ever since I saw one of his videos on Youtube. There's just something so incredibly <i>captivating </i>about him ... he's adorable, funny and besides that he's also very inspiring and creative. This book proves just as much - <b>he shares intimate stories with his readers/viewers and talks openly about the things he learned in life.</b> His school time, relationships, casual hook-ups, his internet presence, different jobs he's had over the years and so much more.<br><br>I have to admit, I never read a biography before nor am I really into nonfiction books but this one might change my opinion about them - especially biographies always seemed very boring to me. This one definitely wasn't and I think what made me love this book so much is that <b>you could totally see/feel/read that this was Tyler Oakley.</b> I mean, everything in this book just screams his name and didn't feel fake or like it's written by someone else. If it was - which I doubt, really - they did a great job. I just felt so connected to him and even could relate to a few things he told us about. It gives (me) hope and shows that even "failures" can lead to something so much better.<br><br><b>The readers got a really deep insight into his life - present and past - and to see that he's just as normal as everyone else actually makes him even more likable.</b> He's been through a lot but still managed to become a happy person and to live life to its fullest. Honestly, I'd love to have a friend like Tyler Oakley ... I mean, who wouldn't? This guy's great and I love him! Also, we can definitely learn a few things from him ... I think I certainly did.<br><br>Fact is, Tyler is an amazing human being and I'm sure with the topics he talks about and all the things he's shared so far, he's helped more than one person. No matter if it is to make them smile, actually learn something or help them through a hard time of their lives - Tyler is inspiring, admirable, intelligent and just an overall interesting person. I'm really glad I read <i>Binge </i>&amp; personally, I think, <b>if you like his Youtube videos or even are just curious/interested in him as a person, you'd surely enjoy this book</b> - it's definitely worth a read!<br><br><a href="http://aworldbetweenfoldedpages.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">www.aworldbetweenfoldedpages.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11484932832997457699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText7197298437946097092" style="display:none">Queen Tyler seriously never fails to disappoint me. Like really, I can't think of a time when he has failed to make me laugh and fall on the floor clutching my stomach.<br />What a great way to start the new year! I have been in a reading slump for 4 months and the new year has made me want to pick up all my unread books at once and just read them all. Of course that's quite impossible so I had to just pick one. <br />Clearly I picked Binge and it was a very good decision. I initially thought this would be a very easy, quick and light read. But I was pleasantly surprised that is was so much more. <br />It had me laughing from the start to end and Tyler also did quite serious chapters which made me really think about the world. Learning about his humble beginnings to where he is today is motivational. </span>

<div id="review_1452961017" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1452961017" />
    <a title="monica kim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/748566-monica-kim"><img alt="monica kim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1545978883p2/748566.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1452961017?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="monica kim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="monica kim" href="/user/show/748566-monica-kim">monica kim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1452961017" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15664584319334522948">I would say this book is primarily for fans of Tyler Oakley. The format isn't anything new (standard celebrity memoir style featuring vignettes and lists) and the writing isn't groundbreaking. However, as a longtime fan, I really enjoyed the read! I went into it expecting a Tyler vlog in book form, but it's so much more emotional and relatable and interesting than that (but don't worry, there are still lots of funny parts too). Also, the book is a huge reminder that even if you've followed someo</span>
  <span id="freeText15664584319334522948" style="display:none">I would say this book is primarily for fans of Tyler Oakley. The format isn't anything new (standard celebrity memoir style featuring vignettes and lists) and the writing isn't groundbreaking. However, as a longtime fan, I really enjoyed the read! I went into it expecting a Tyler vlog in book form, but it's so much more emotional and relatable and interesting than that (but don't worry, there are still lots of funny parts too). Also, the book is a huge reminder that even if you've followed someone's entire social media presence, you still really don't know anything about them. So yeah, if you're a fan of Tyler Oakley, definitely pick it up. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15664584319334522948" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1421939345" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1421939345" />
    <a title="Erin Calder" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31975369-erin-calder"><img alt="Erin Calder" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1445448024p2/31975369.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1421939345?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin Calder" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin Calder" href="/user/show/31975369-erin-calder">Erin Calder</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1421939345" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6623185884617034559">I’ve just read the final sentence of my signed copy of Binge, and put down said book for the first time since picking it up. What better time to write a book review than seconds after finishing the book, with tear-tracks still noticeable on your face and a distinct aching in your heart?<br/><br/>Tyler Oakley is someone who means a lot to me, as his shared video experiences have helped me vastly throughout the (roughly) three years I have been watching his content. Thanks to the wonderful online community </span>
  <span id="freeText6623185884617034559" style="display:none">I’ve just read the final sentence of my signed copy of Binge, and put down said book for the first time since picking it up. What better time to write a book review than seconds after finishing the book, with tear-tracks still noticeable on your face and a distinct aching in your heart?<br /><br />Tyler Oakley is someone who means a lot to me, as his shared video experiences have helped me vastly throughout the (roughly) three years I have been watching his content. Thanks to the wonderful online community that he has helped to create, I have made at least four of my closest friends, three of whom I have met in real life, all thanks to him.<br /><br />Consequently, it was without question that I ordered Binge. I’m not sure exactly what I was expecting, but I know that it wasn’t this. Never before have I felt so close to him, as though I’ve seen hours of his life on my computer screen -and even had the opportunity to hug him at his London Slumber Party tour stop-, he has truly never shared such intimately personal details of his life with me or any subscriber. <br /><br />It was a worry of mine that I wouldn’t feel the same connection with Tyler that I usually do whilst reading this book. Thankfully, this was far from the case. Throughout, it felt as if he was speaking to me still, as near as he has always been with videos, closer, even. His unique way of phrasing his sentences, creating inside jokes -perhaps unknowingly- and just talking to us like equals has been built upon and yet stayed true to itself throughout Binge. Not a shred of his distinctive personality has been lost, although it has definitely shone through stronger than ever before.<br /><br />Now, as always, I am truly proud to call myself one of his people. I love Tyler with all of my heart.<br /><br />-Erin (@fandomasfuck on twitter and tumblr)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6623185884617034559" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1576486416" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1576486416" />
    <a title="Linda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1740304-linda"><img alt="Linda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1344432666p2/1740304.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1576486416?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Linda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Linda" href="/user/show/1740304-linda">Linda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1740304-linda?shelf=audio-only">audio-only</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1740304-linda?shelf=because-my-daughter-is-reading-it">because-my-daughter-is-reading-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1740304-linda?shelf=memoir">memoir</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1576486416" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6448274523618174438">I am not the target audience. I'm a middle aged computer professional who does not follow anyone on youTube or Twitter. I had never heard of Tyler Oakley.<br/><br/>My daughter, however, spends a great deal of her free time watching YouTube. When I have watched some of the shows she watches, I generally find them insipid and annoying. (I won't name names.)<br/><br/>This is the second YouTuber book she's asked to read. I decided to read (listen to) it along with her.<br/><br/>My first thought is, this is totally inappropriate </span>
  <span id="freeText6448274523618174438" style="display:none">I am not the target audience. I'm a middle aged computer professional who does not follow anyone on youTube or Twitter. I had never heard of Tyler Oakley.<br /><br />My daughter, however, spends a great deal of her free time watching YouTube. When I have watched some of the shows she watches, I generally find them insipid and annoying. (I won't name names.)<br /><br />This is the second YouTuber book she's asked to read. I decided to read (listen to) it along with her.<br /><br />My first thought is, this is totally inappropriate for an adolescent. Porn, alcohol, eating disorders, depression, coming out, fitting in, casual sex, heartbreak, pot brownies at summer camp, hangovers with projectile vomiting, abuse, profanity, fetishes, and more. <br /><br />On the other hand, Tyler handles all these topics with a great deal of heart, honesty, humor, and despite his suggestions to the contrary, humility. He's quite wise for such a young man, and there are a lot of lessons learned he shares along the way. When his mother (I love the relationship he has with his mom!) adeptly teaches him a little humility after his rant in the T-Mobile store. When he learns the hard way, as many of us do, not to give up too much of yourself in a lopsided relationship. When the Trevor Project hands him a life line, and he pays it forward. And on and on. <br /><br />Rather than shielding my daughter from these messy life lessons, I choose to use them as talking points. She will have her own lessons to learn in the coming years, and I hope she has the support to get through them, and the wisdom to learn from them. As this guy has. <br /><br />I might even watch his YouTube channel now and again. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6448274523618174438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('33LteJZEybeOYwZqB7TN9ZuaqRUrSjqzRlrNfvTo+lmWns2HwjRzprtlaGgYQchQS4+7GIKVyXmKwGW6Dnho5A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('m0wu7Z6Q1XFF7H8JCgDAWZWvW1w9/rJQRQoBALtBbofSoA4SyuBvYHDqEQsV9cX8RbpJUZQhQZqJkKnEQdH8Og==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer17510064228496102886">Michigan native and pop-culture tastemaker Tyler Oakley has amassed more than 21 million social media followers through his humorous, no-holds-barred YouTube videos, high-profile interviews, and social rights advocacy. After uploading his first video eight years ago, Oakley took the Internet by storm. With successes ranging from interviews with First Lady Michelle Obama and boy band One Direction;</span>
  <span id="freeText17510064228496102886" style="display:none">Michigan native and pop-culture tastemaker Tyler Oakley has amassed more than 21 million social media followers through his humorous, no-holds-barred YouTube videos, high-profile interviews, and social rights advocacy. After uploading his first video eight years ago, Oakley took the Internet by storm. With successes ranging from interviews with First Lady Michelle Obama and boy band One Direction; a worldwide, multi-city live tour; and a record-breaking social media following, Oakley is a YouTube icon. He lives in Los Angeles, California, where he uploads weekly videos from his living room.</span>
